### [183] [CogGen: Cognitive-Load-Informed Fully Unsupervised Deep Generative Modeling for Compressively Sampled MRI Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04438)
*Qingyong Zhu,Yumin Tan,Xiang Gu,Dong Liang*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: CogGen是一种认知负荷感知的无监督深度生成模型，通过渐进式调度内在难度和外部干扰来改善压缩感知MRI重建，使用从易到难的k空间加权/选择策略，相比传统方法提升了保真度和收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统无监督深度生成模型（如DIP和INR）在压缩感知MRI中依赖架构先验，但病态逆问题通常需要大量迭代且容易过拟合测量噪声，需要更有效的训练策略。

Method: 提出CogGen框架，将CS-MRI视为分阶段反演，通过渐进式调度内在难度（k空间频率）和外部干扰（噪声）来调节认知负荷。采用从易到难的k空间加权/选择策略：早期迭代强调低频、高信噪比、结构主导的样本，后期引入高频或噪声主导的测量。通过自定步调课程学习实现，包含学生模式（模型当前能学习的内容）和教师模式（应遵循的内容）标准。

Result: 实验和分析表明，CogGen-DIP和CogGen-INR在保真度和收敛性方面优于强大的无监督基线方法和有竞争力的监督流程。

Conclusion: CogGen通过认知负荷感知的渐进式训练策略，有效解决了传统无监督深度生成模型在压缩感知MRI中的过拟合和收敛问题，为有限训练数据或计算资源下的医学图像重建提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Fully unsupervised deep generative modeling (FU-DGM) is promising for compressively sampled MRI (CS-MRI) when training data or compute are limited. Classical FU-DGMs such as DIP and INR rely on architectural priors, but the ill-conditioned inverse problem often demands many iterations and easily overfits measurement noise. We propose CogGen, a cognitive-load-informed FU-DGM that casts CS-MRI as staged inversion and regulates task-side "cognitive load" by progressively scheduling intrinsic difficulty and extraneous interference. CogGen replaces uniform data fitting with an easy-to-hard k-space weighting/selection strategy: early iterations emphasize low-frequency, high-SNR, structure-dominant samples, while higher-frequency or noise-dominated measurements are introduced later. We realize this schedule via self-paced curriculum learning with complementary student-mode (what the model can currently learn) and teacher-mode (what it should follow) criteria, supporting both soft weighting and hard selection. Experiments and analysis show that CogGen-DIP and CogGen-INR improve fidelity and convergence over strong unsupervised baselines and competitive supervised pipelines.

</details>


### [184] [Anti-Aliasing Snapshot HDR Imaging Using Non-Regular Sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05133)
*Teresa Stürzenhofäcker,Moritz Klimm,Jürgen Seiler,André Kaup*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于空间变化孔径的瞬态HDR成像传感器，通过组合两种不同尺寸的像素原型来扩展动态范围，并采用非规则像素排列来减少混叠效应，最终在傅里叶域进行重建以恢复高细节图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 瞬态HDR成像对于在单次曝光中捕捉场景的完整动态范围至关重要，特别是在视频和动态环境中，运动使得多曝光技术或复杂硬件设置无法使用。现有方法在空间分辨率损失和混叠效应方面存在限制。

Method: 1. 设计基于空间变化孔径的瞬态HDR成像传感器，结合两种不同尺寸的像素原型（大像素和小像素）；2. 采用非规则像素排列来减轻混叠效应并克服大像素带来的空间分辨率损失；3. 在傅里叶域进行图像重建，利用自然图像在频域中的稀疏表示来恢复高细节图像。

Result: 通过模拟和分析，结果表明所提出的非规则HDR传感器布局能够有效获取高动态范围图像，同时避免了混叠伪影，在空间分辨率方面表现良好。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的基于空间变化孔径和非规则像素排列的瞬态HDR成像传感器是一种有效的方法，能够在单次曝光中获取高质量的高动态范围图像，特别适用于视频和动态环境应用。

Abstract: Snapshot HDR imaging is essential to capture the full dynamic range of a scene in a single exposure, making it essential for video and dynamic environments where motion prevents the use of multi-exposure techniques or complex hardware set-ups. This work presents a snapshot HDR imaging sensor that is based on spatially varying apertures, implemented by combining two differently sized prototype pixels. The different light integration areas physically extend the dynamic range towards the lower end, compared to a standard high resolution sensor. A non-regular pixel arrangement is suggested, to mitigate aliasing and overcome a loss in spatial resolution that is associated with increased light integration area of the larger prototype pixel. Subsequent reconstruction in the Fourier domain, where natural images can be sparsely represented allows to recover the image with high detail. The image acquisition approach with the proposed non-regular HDR sensor is simulated and analysed with special emphasis on the spatial resolution. The results suggest the snapshot HDR sensor layout to be an effective way to acquire images with high dynamic range and free from aliasing artefacts.

### [185] [Limited-Angle CT Reconstruction Using Multi-Volume Latent Consistency Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05183)
*Hinako Isogai,Naruki Murahashi,Mitsuhiro Nakamura,Megumi Nakao*

Main category: eess.IV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出多体积潜在扩散模型，使用从多个有效视野获得的三维潜在表示作为有限角度CT重建的指导。通过将一致性模型引入潜在空间实现快速稳定推理，通过多体积编码器从全局区域和中心区域的不同尺度获取潜在变量，实现在不同FOV条件下高精度保持器官边界信息和内部结构。

Conclusion: 该方法相比现有方法实现了高精度合成CT图像生成，在不同视野条件下保持器官边界和内部结构，对临床实践中多样化的成像条件具有适用性，证实了在未知投影角度条件下的稳定重建能力。

Abstract: Limited-angle computed tomography (LACT) reconstruction is an inverse problem with severe ill-posedness arising from missing projection angles, and it is difficult to restore high-precision images without sufficient prior knowledge. In recent years, machine learning methods represented by diffusion models have demonstrated high image generation capabilities. However, accurate restoration of three-dimensional structures of organs and vessels and preservation of contrast remain challenges, and the impact of differences in diverse clinical imaging conditions such as field of view (FOV) and projection angle range on reconstruction accuracy has not been sufficiently investigated.
  In this study, we propose a multi-volume latent diffusion model that uses three-dimensional latent representations obtained from multiple effective fields of view as guidance for LACT reconstruction in clinical practical problems. The proposed method achieves fast and stable inference by introducing consistency models into latent space, and enables high-precision preservation of organ boundary information and internal structures under different FOV conditions through a Multi-volume encoder that acquires latent variables from different scales of the global region and central region.
  The evaluation experiments demonstrated that the proposed method achieved high-precision synthetic CT image generation compared to existing methods. Under the limited-angle condition of 60 degrees, MAE of 10.12 HU and SSIM of 0.9677 were achieved, and under the extreme limited-angle condition of 30 degrees, MAE of 16.69 HU and SSIM of 0.9393 were achieved. Furthermore, stable reconstruction performance was demonstrated even for unknown projection angle conditions not included during training, confirming the applicability to diverse imaging conditions in clinical practice.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数据存储介质寿命短且存储需求激增，DNA存储具有高密度、长寿命和低能耗优势，但当前DNA存储面临成本高、可靠性差的问题，且缺乏有效的随机访问机制，导致读取特定文件时需要测序所有寡核苷酸，成本高昂。

Method: 基于JPEG2000渐进式解码功能，将图像的不同分辨率层分别编码为DNA寡核苷酸序列，使用JPEG DNA VM编解码器确保高可靠性。通过纳米孔测序仪的自适应采样方法，在测序时按需选择特定寡核苷酸进行测序和解码，实现PCR-free的随机访问。

Result: 系统能够根据所需分辨率调整需要测序和解码的寡核苷酸集合，显著降低读取成本，同时保持高可靠性，为DNA存储的实用化提供了可行方案。

Conclusion: 该DNA图像存储系统通过渐进式编码和自适应采样技术，有效解决了DNA存储中的随机访问问题，降低了读取成本，推动了DNA存储技术向实用化和经济可行性发展。

Abstract: The short lifespan of traditional data storage media, coupled with an exponential increase in storage demand, has made long-term archival a fundamental problem in the data storage industry and beyond. Consequently, researchers are looking for innovative media solutions that can store data over long time periods at a very low cost. DNA molecules, with their high density, long lifespan, and low energy needs, have emerged as a viable alternative to digital data archival. However, current DNA data storage technologies are facing challenges with respect to cost and reliability. Thus, coding rate and error robustness are critical to scale DNA storage and make it technologically and economically achievable. Moreover, the molecules of DNA that encode different files are often located in the same oligo pool. Without random access solutions at the oligo level, it is very impractical to decode a specific file from these mixed pools, as all oligos need to first be sequenced and decoded before a target file can be retrieved, which greatly deteriorates the read cost.
  This paper introduces a solution to efficiently encode and store images into DNA molecules, that aims at reducing the read cost necessary to retrieve a resolution-reduced version of an image. This image storage system is based on the Progressive Decoding Functionality of the JPEG2000 codec but can be adapted to any conventional progressive codec. Each resolution layer is encoded into a set of oligos using the JPEG DNA VM codec, a DNA-based coder that aims at retrieving a file with a high reliability. Depending on the desired resolution to be read, the set of oligos as well as the portion of the oligos to be sequenced and decoded are adjusted accordingly. These oligos will be selected at sequencing time, with the help of the adaptive sampling method provided by the Nanopore sequencers, making it a PCR-free random access solution.

</details>


<div id='q-fin.PM'></div>

# q-fin.PM [[Back]](#toc)

### [187] [Explainable Regime Aware Investing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04441)
*Amine Boukardagha*

Main category: q-fin.PM

TL;DR: 提出基于严格因果Wasserstein隐马尔可夫模型的可解释性制度感知投资组合构建框架，通过动态适应制度复杂性并保持稳定经济解释，在多样化跨资产日度数据上实现显著更高的风险调整后收益和更低的最大回撤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统投资组合方法难以动态适应市场制度变化，缺乏对制度转换的稳定识别和解释性。需要一种既能动态调整制度复杂性，又能保持经济解释稳定性的框架，以提升投资组合的稳健性和风险控制能力。

Method: 结合滚动高斯HMM推断、预测性模型阶数选择和基于模板的身份追踪（使用高斯分量间的2-Wasserstein距离）。将制度概率嵌入考虑交易成本的均值-方差优化框架，并在多样化日度跨资产数据上进行评估。

Result: 相对于等权重和SPX买入持有基准，Wasserstein HMM获得显著更高的风险调整后表现（夏普比率2.18 vs 1.59和1.18），最大回撤大幅降低（-5.43% vs -14.62%）。在2025年初的"解放日"股市抛售期间，策略动态降低股票敞口并转向防御性资产，减轻了峰值到谷值的损失。

Conclusion: 制度推断稳定性，特别是身份保持和自适应复杂性控制，是日度资产配置中投资组合回撤和实施稳健性的首要决定因素。参数化制度模型相比非参数KNN条件矩估计器产生显著更低的换手率和更平滑的权重演变。

Abstract: We propose an explainable regime-aware portfolio construction framework based on a strictly causal Wasserstein Hidden Markov Model. The model combines rolling Gaussian HMM inference with predictive model-order selection and template-based identity tracking using the 2-Wasserstein distance between Gaussian components. This allows regime complexity to adapt dynamically while preserving stable economic interpretation. Regime probabilities are embedded into a transaction-cost-aware mean-variance optimization framework and evaluated on a diversified daily cross-asset universe. Relative to equal-weight and SPX buy-and-hold benchmarks, the Wasserstein HMM achieves materially higher risk-adjusted performance with Sharpe ratios of 2.18 versus 1.59 and 1.18 and substantially lower maximum drawdown of negative 5.43 percent versus negative 14.62 percent for SPX. During the early 2025 equity selloff labeled Liberation Day, the strategy dynamically reduced equity exposure and shifted toward defensive assets, mitigating peak-to-trough losses. Compared to a nonparametric KNN conditional-moment estimator using the same features and optimization layer, the parametric regime model produces materially lower turnover and smoother weight evolution. The results demonstrate that regime inference stability, particularly identity preservation and adaptive complexity control, is a first-order determinant of portfolio drawdown and implementation robustness in daily asset allocation.

</details>


<div id='cs.MM'></div>

# cs.MM [[Back]](#toc)

### [188] [SarcasmMiner: A Dual-Track Post-Training Framework for Robust Audio-Visual Sarcasm Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05275)
*Zhu Li,Yongjian Chen,Huiyuan Lai,Xiyuan Gao,Shekhar Nayak,Matt Coler*

Main category: cs.MM

TL;DR: SarcasmMiner：基于强化学习的后训练框架，通过结构化推理和双重轨迹蒸馏策略提升多模态讽刺检测性能，在MUStARD++数据集上F1从59.83%提升至70.22%


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态讽刺检测需要解决文本、声学和视觉线索之间的语用不一致性，现有基础模型在多模态推理中存在幻觉问题，需要更鲁棒的推理方法

Method: 提出SarcasmMiner强化学习后训练框架：1）将讽刺检测重构为结构化推理；2）采用双重轨迹蒸馏策略：高质量教师轨迹初始化学生模型，完整轨迹训练生成式奖励模型评估推理质量；3）使用组相对策略优化和分离的准确性与推理质量奖励优化学生模型

Result: 在MUStARD++数据集上，SarcasmMiner将F1分数从零样本的59.83%、监督微调的68.23%提升至70.22%，推理感知的奖励建模增强了性能和跨模态基础

Conclusion: SarcasmMiner通过强化学习后训练和结构化推理方法有效提升了多模态讽刺检测性能，推理感知的奖励建模能够同时改善模型性能和跨模态基础能力

Abstract: Multimodal sarcasm detection requires resolving pragmatic incongruity across textual, acoustic, and visual cues through cross-modal reasoning. To enable robust sarcasm reasoning with foundation models, we propose SarcasmMiner, a reinforcement learning based post-training framework that resists hallucination in multimodal reasoning. We reformulate sarcasm detection as structured reasoning and adopt a dual-track distillation strategy: high-quality teacher trajectories initialize the student model, while the full set of trajectories trains a generative reward model (GenRM) to evaluate reasoning quality. The student is optimized with group relative policy optimization (GRPO) using decoupled rewards for accuracy and reasoning quality. On MUStARD++, SarcasmMiner increases F1 from 59.83% (zero-shot), 68.23% (supervised finetuning) to 70.22%. These findings suggest that reasoning-aware reward modeling enhances both performance and multimodal grounding.

</details>
